name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Family Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted February 15, 2024
msg:During the Spring Festival self-driving trip, I stayed at this hotel and the overall experience was very satisfactory. In terms of service facilities, the hotel has the facilities of a five-star hotel, but it may have been built earlier, and the overall design style is more classic, which is more popular among parents of the same age group.

The most satisfying thing is the hotel's service and breakfast. Staying during the Spring Festival, the hotel has sufficient service personnel in all aspects. Whether it is the concierge, front desk, guest room, or restaurant staff, they are all energetic. Everyone has a sincere smile on their face, making people feel at home. When accommodation encounters problems, various depar**ents actively cooperate and respond quickly. As guests, we feel like we are living in a big family. There is a feeling that the leaders and managers of this hotel should take good care of their employees.

In addition, this hotel is very good at catering. Wedding banquets, birthday banquets, and family dinners were seen every day during our stay. The flow of passengers coming and going every day was quite large. The hotel has a wide range of restaurants. In addition to banquets, there are also Chinese restaurants, Japanese restaurants, and all-day buffet restaurants. The breakfast in the buffet restaurant is rich in variety and replenished in a timely manner. The fruits and vegetables are very fresh and the rest of the meals taste good. I personally particularly like the coffee here. The preparation is moderate and the taste is appropriate. You can feel the restaurant manager and chef's meticulousness in the details.

The only drawback is that the room we stayed in was a bit hot, which may be related to the sharp rise in temperature in the past two days. In the morning after the first night, I happened to meet the aunt who was cleaning the guest rooms. After reporting the situation to her, the aunt specially left a few extra bottles of water in our room. Feel it here again
Every employee strives to provide guests with better service within their own capabilities.

Generally speaking, it is highly recommended. I hope that such a good hotel will get better and better, business will be prosperous, and wealth will be prosperous!
